### Level 0 - Foundational

#### Fake Horcrux

An object made to resemble a Horcrux as a deception, used to mislead Dark wizards about the true location of soul fragments.

**Also known as:** Decoy Horcrux

#### Horcrux

A dark magical object created by splitting one's soul and embedding a fragment of it into an object, thereby granting a form of immortality; destroying all Horcruxes is necessary to defeat the creator.

**Also known as:** Dark Magical Object, Horcruxes (plural), Horcruxes, Soul fragment object

**Tags:** magical object, dark magic, Harry Potter universe, Magic Objects, Harry Potter Lore, Harry Potter, Magic Artifacts, magic, immortality, wizardry, artifact, magical objects, soul magic, Defensive Magic, Magical Dark Arts, Magic Theory

**Related:** Fake Horcrux, Voldemort's Horcruxes

#### Inferi

Inferi are reanimated corpses controlled through dark magic, capable of physical attack but lacking independent will, often used as guardians or instruments of terror.

**Also known as:** animated corpses, Reanimated Corpses

**Tags:** magical creatures, dark magic, Harry Potter universe, Creatures, Magic

**Related:** Enchanted Coins, Defense Against The Dark Arts (D.A.)

#### Occlumens

An Occlumens is a witch or wizard skilled in Occlumency, the magical art of shielding one's mind against external penetration and influence, particularly to protect against Legilimency.

**Tags:** magic, defensive magic, Harry Potter lore

#### Seeker

A player position in the wizarding sport of Quidditch whose main objective is to catch the Golden Snitch, thereby ending the game and earning their team significant points.

**Tags:** Sports, Quidditch, Positions

**Prerequisites:** Quidditch Cup

**Related:** Quidditch

---

#### Detention tasks at Hogwarts

Punitive duties assigned during detention that can include menial or tedious tasks such as copying old records by hand without magic.

**Also known as:** Detention work

**Tags:** Discipline, Harry Potter universe, Hogwarts

**Prerequisites:** Apprehended Using an Illegal Hex

**Related:** Hogwarts wrongdoers’ records, Filch

#### Unicorn Hair

A magical substance commonly used as a core ingredient in wands and potions valued for its purity and magical properties.

**Tags:** magic, magical substance, Harry Potter

**Prerequisites:** Potion

**Related:** Defense Against The Dark Arts (D.A.)

#### Langlock Spell

A magical hex that temporarily glues the target's tongue to the roof of their mouth, preventing them from speaking.

**Tags:** spells, curse, Harry Potter universe

**Prerequisites:** Defense Against the Dark Arts Class

**Related:** Jinxes and Hexes

**Prerequisites:** Tom Riddle senior

A medium-denomination coin in the wizarding currency system, subordinate to Galleons but above Knuts.

**Tags:** currency, wizarding economy

**Prerequisites:** Knut

#### Galleons

The main unit of currency in the wizarding world, used to purchase goods and services.

A hidden shopping area in the wizarding world where witches and wizards buy magical supplies, including joke shops such as Fred and George’s business location.

**Related:** Slug Club

**Tags:** rules, punishment, education

**Prerequisites:** Magical Law

**Related:** Phineas Nigellus, Filch

#### Magic Control

Magic control is the taught discipline of managing and consciously directing magical powers to avoid unintended consequences or misuse of magic.

**Also known as:** controlling magic

**Tags:** magic, education, self-discipline

**Prerequisites:** Wizarding Wand

**Related:** Half-Blood Prince’s Book

---

#### Blood Traitor

A pejorative term used by pure-blood supremacists to describe wizards of pure-blood descent who associate with Muggle-borns or oppose pure-blood ideology.

**Tags:** wizarding society, culture, Harry Potter universe

**Prerequisites:** Blood Purity

**Related:** Magical Law

The grading system for O.W.L. exams, including Outstanding (O), Exceeds Expectations (E), Acceptable (A), Poor (P), Dreadful (D), and Troll (T).

**Also known as:** wizarding exam grades

**Tags:** education, wizarding world, assessment

### Level 2 - Intermediate

#### Concealed Entrance

A hidden or magically obscured gateway within the cave wall that blocks access until activated or revealed.

**Prerequisites:** Underwater Passage

**Related:** Lord Voldemort’s Obstacles in the Cave

---

#### Diary Horcrux

A specific Horcrux in the form of a diary containing a fragment of Voldemort's soul, which could possess others and was intended as a weapon and safeguard.

**Also known as:** Riddle’s diary

**Tags:** Horcrux, dark magic, artifact, wizardry

**Prerequisites:** Soul

**Related:** Memory Modification

---

#### Silver Dagger (flat side usage)

A silver dagger used in potion-making; crushing ingredients with its flat side releases more potent juice than cutting.

**Tags:** tools, potions

**Prerequisites:** Potion Stirring Directions (Clockwise and Counterclockwise)

---

#### Summons (Wizarding Legal Document)

A formal written notice commanding a wizard to appear before the Ministry of Magic for a hearing related to a breach of wizarding law.

**Also known as:** Magical Summons

**Tags:** legal document, wizarding law, Harry Potter universe

**Prerequisites:** Hearing (Wizarding Legal Process)

---

#### Chosen One

The term 'Chosen One' refers to Harry Potter, who survived the Killing Curse as a baby and is prophesied to have extraordinary powers to defeat Voldemort.

**Tags:** prophecy, Harry Potter, character role, destiny, wizardry, characters, prophecies, Harry Potter lore

**Prerequisites:** Prophecy (Harry Potter)

---

#### Galleon

A Galleon is a gold coin and the primary currency used in the wizarding world for purchasing goods and services.

**Tags:** currency, wizarding economy, wizarding currency, economics, Harry Potter lore

**Prerequisites:** Sickle

**Related:** Diagon Alley

---

#### Potions Grade Requirements for Auror

A minimum grade in Potions O.W.L. exams is required for the Auror career path within the wizarding world, reflecting the importance of potion knowledge in the role.

**Tags:** education, career requirements, wizarding world

**Prerequisites:** O.W.L. Grades

---

#### N.E.W.T.

Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test; advanced level magical examinations taken after O.W.L.s, required for certain career paths in the wizarding world.

**Also known as:** Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test

**Tags:** education, wizarding world, exam

**Prerequisites:** Potions Class

**Related:** Hogwarts Houses

---

#### Apparition Test

The Apparition Test is a standardized magical examination at Hogwarts allowing witches and wizards aged seventeen or older to learn and practice apparition, the magical ability to teleport instantaneously.

**Also known as:** Apparition License Test, Magical teleportation test, Apparition Proficiency Test

**Tags:** magic skill, exam, Harry Potter, wizarding education, magic, testing, Harry Potter universe, Education, Transportation, Skills Testing

**Prerequisites:** Apparition, Wilkie Twycross

---

#### Antidote

A potion or substance used to counteract the effects of a poison.

**Also known as:** Cure, Counterpoison

**Tags:** potion-making, magic, poison treatment

**Prerequisites:** Poison, Golpalott’s Third Law

**Related:** Potions

---

#### Baby Tom Riddle's Behavior

Tom Riddle as a baby was described as not crying much and being 'odd' as he grew older, suggesting unusual or atypical early childhood behavior.

**Also known as:** Tom Riddle as a baby

**Tags:** character development, child behavior, Harry Potter lore

**Prerequisites:** Merope Riddle, Orphanage

---

#### Cursed

To be cursed is to be afflicted by a magical spell intended to cause harm, misfortune, or a lasting negative effect on a person or object.

**Also known as:** Hexed, Jinxed

**Tags:** magic, spell effects

**Prerequisites:** Magic Control, Smallest Possible Amount of Skin

**Related:** Dark Wizard

---

#### Defense Against the Dark Arts O.W.L.

The Defense Against the Dark Arts O.W.L. is an Ordinary Wizarding Level standardized test assessing a student's proficiency in defensive magic against dark forces.

**Also known as:** DADA O.W.L.

**Tags:** Harry Potter academics, Examinations, Defense magic

**Prerequisites:** Occlumency, Episkey, Essence of Rue

**Related:** Unbreakable Vow, Rotfang Conspiracy

---

A magical plant ingredient used in potion-making that releases juice when crushed and affects the potion's properties.

**Tags:** Harry Potter, potion ingredients, magical plants

**Prerequisites:** Silver Dagger (flat side usage)
